  1088. # [10:22] * padenot|pto|away is now known as padenot|pto

  1091. # [10:25] <avih> and all those affect the animation. i want to measure when things stop affecting the animation. so onload or some other arbitrary event doesn't necessarily convey that point in time
  1092. # [10:25] * Joins: edmorley (uid27002@moz-5F4AA75A.irccloud.com)

  1102. # [10:28] * Joins: jfkthame (jfkthame@CED678F6.9435D87F.3E2A4E92.IP)
